### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with $SkillName or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
1) After deciding to use a skill, open its SKILL.md. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
2) When SKILL.md references relative paths (e.g., scripts/foo.py), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
3) If SKILL.md points to extra folders such as references/, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
4) If scripts/ exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
5) If assets/ or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
- If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
- Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
- Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
- Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from SKILL.md unless you're blocked.
- When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.

## Instruction Priority

Superpowers skills override default system prompt behavior, but **user instructions always take precedence**:

1. **User's explicit instructions** (CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, AGENTS.md, direct requests) 鈥?highest priority
2. **Superpowers skills** 鈥?override default system behavior where they conflict
3. **Default system prompt** 鈥?lowest priority

If CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, or AGENTS.md says "don't use TDD" and a skill says "always use TDD," follow the user's instructions. The user is in control.

## How to Access Skills

**In Claude Code:** Use the `Skill` tool. When you invoke a skill, its content is loaded and presented to you鈥攆ollow it directly. Never use the Read tool on skill files.

**In Gemini CLI:** Skills activate via the `activate_skill` tool. Gemini loads skill metadata at session start and activates the full content on demand.

**In other environments:** Check your platform's documentation for how skills are loaded.

## Platform Adaptation

Skills use Claude Code tool names. Non-CC platforms: see `references/codex-tools.md` (Codex) for tool equivalents. Gemini CLI users get the tool mapping loaded automatically via GEMINI.md.

# Using Skills

## The Rule

**Invoke relevant or requested skills BEFORE any response or action.** Even a 1% chance a skill might apply means that you should invoke the skill to check. If an invoked skill turns out to be wrong for the situation, you don't need to use it.

```dot
digraph skill_flow {
    "User message received" [shape=doublecircle];
    "About to EnterPlanMode?" [shape=doublecircle];
    "Already brainstormed?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" [shape=box];
    "Might any skill apply?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke Skill tool" [shape=box];
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" [shape=box];
    "Has checklist?" [shape=diamond];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [shape=box];
    "Follow skill exactly" [shape=box];
    "Respond (including clarifications)" [shape=doublecircle];

    "About to EnterPlanMode?" -> "Already brainstormed?";
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Invoke brainstorming skill" [label="no"];
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Might any skill apply?" [label="yes"];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" -> "Might any skill apply?";

    "User message received" -> "Might any skill apply?";
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Invoke Skill tool" [label="yes, even 1%"];
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Respond (including clarifications)" [label="definitely not"];
    "Invoke Skill tool" -> "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'";
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" -> "Has checklist?";
    "Has checklist?" -> "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [label="yes"];
    "Has checklist?" -> "Follow skill exactly" [label="no"];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" -> "Follow skill exactly";
}
```

## Red Flags

These thoughts mean STOP鈥攜ou're rationalizing:

| Thought | Reality |
|---------|---------|
| "This is just a simple question" | Questions are tasks. Check for skills. |
| "I need more context first" | Skill check comes BEFORE clarifying questions. |
| "Let me explore the codebase first" | Skills tell you HOW to explore. Check first. |
| "I can check git/files quickly" | Files lack conversation context. Check for skills. |
| "Let me gather information first" | Skills tell you HOW to gather information. |
| "This doesn't need a formal skill" | If a skill exists, use it. |
| "I remember this skill" | Skills evolve. Read current version. |
| "This doesn't count as a task" | Action = task. Check for skills. |
| "The skill is overkill" | Simple things become complex. Use it. |
| "I'll just do this one thing first" | Check BEFORE doing anything. |
| "This feels productive" | Undisciplined action wastes time. Skills prevent this. |
| "I know what that means" | Knowing the concept 鈮?using the skill. Invoke it. |

## Skill Priority

When multiple skills could apply, use this order:

1. **Process skills first** (brainstorming, debugging) - these determine HOW to approach the task
2. **Implementation skills second** (frontend-design, mcp-builder) - these guide execution

"Let's build X" 鈫?brainstorming first, then implementation skills.
"Fix this bug" 鈫?debugging first, then domain-specific skills.

## Skill Types

**Rigid** (TDD, debugging): Follow exactly. Don't adapt away discipline.

**Flexible** (patterns): Adapt principles to context.

The skill itself tells you which.

## User Instructions

Instructions say WHAT, not HOW. "Add X" or "Fix Y" doesn't mean skip workflows.

## 进行中
- OpenClaw 结果消费层：已在仓库内提供 `openclaw_result` 标准结果对象、本地客户端/CLI、以及 workspace skill + PowerShell wrapper；下一步转向用户实际 OpenClaw 工作区/频道中的最终使用方式固化，而不再依赖人工记忆调用参数。
- P0 第二批收口：在真实跑通老 `pre` 生产链后，继续识别 `stage8/stage9` 的全局副作用与产物命名差异，避免 OpenClaw 侧消费时还要自行去重或猜测主产物。
- API/队列稳定性收口：当前未启 Redis 时，`WorkerService` 仍走 in-memory registry/queue；虽然本轮已修复 API 启动漏掉 `service.start()` 导致任务永远卡在 `pending` 的问题，但 API 进程重启后仍无法恢复内存态任务，后续需决定是补本地恢复逻辑还是正式启 Redis。
- 性能收口优先项：先处理老 `pre` 流水线“每任务重启子进程 + 重导入 + 重新预热模型”的固定冷启动开销，目标是改成常驻预热的独立 runner 进程池，并保留当前 `subprocess` 方案作为兜底回退。

## 当前阶段结论
- 方案B已确定为当前执行路线：以 `domain/video/pipeline.py` + `domain/video/stages/` 作为唯一生产主链，禁止旧架构级兜底，禁止长期双轨运行。
- 当前阻塞点不是 OpenClaw 接口层，而是内置视频流水线本体未完成：`domain/video/pipeline.py` 依赖的 `domain/video/stages/` 缺失。
- 上一阶段成果已独立提交并推送：`9a0d91a feat: add warm internal pipeline runner`。
- Redis 继续采用宿主机服务化方式，不以 Docker 部署为未来前提。
- 当前测试已锁定的 `strict_rejected`、`timeline_fallback`、`copy_fallback`、`rule_based` 等行为，在等价替代契约落地前继续按正式运行时保护处理，不视为旧架构兜底。
- OpenClaw 只是第一层 skill 适配平台，不是系统唯一宿主；方案B新增明确三层结构：平台无关核心能力层、API/CLI 通用入口层、Skill/Wrapper 适配层。

     def _resolve_forum_upload_config(self) -> Dict[str, str]:
         base_url = str(os.getenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "")).strip()
         username = str(os.getenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "")).strip()
         password = str(os.getenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "")).strip()
         if base_url and username and password:
             return {"base_url": base_url, "username": username, "password": password}
 
         loaded = self._load_forum_upload_config_from_file(self.forum_settings_path)
         return {
             "base_url": base_url or loaded.get("base_url", ""),
             "username": username or loaded.get("username", ""),
             "password": password or loaded.get("password", ""),
         }
 
     def _load_forum_upload_config_from_file(self, path_text: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
         path = Path(str(path_text or "").strip())
         if not path.exists():
             return {}
         try:
             import yaml  # type: ignore
         except Exception:
             return {}
 
         try:
             payload = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")) or {}
         except Exception:
             return {}
         if not isinstance(payload, dict):
             return {}
         main_forum = (payload.get("forums") or {}).get("main", {})
         credentials = payload.get("credentials", {})
         if not isinstance(main_forum, dict):
             main_forum = {}
         if not isinstance(credentials, dict):
             credentials = {}
         return {
             "base_url": str(main_forum.get("base_url", "")).strip(),
             "username": str(credentials.get("username", "")).strip(),
             "password": str(credentials.get("password", "")).strip(),
         }
 
     def _is_retryable_forum_error(self, error_message: str) -> bool:
         text = str(error_message or "").strip().lower()
         if not text:
             return False
         statuses = [int(item) for item in re.findall(r"status\s*=?\s*(\d{3})", text)]
         if any(400 <= status < 500 for status in statuses):
             return False
         if any(status >= 500 for status in statuses):
             return True
         if "login failed" in text or "auth" in text or "permission" in text:
             return False
         transient_markers = (
             "timeout",
             "timed out",
             "connection",
             "network",
             "temporar",
             "exception",
             "status=0",
         )
         return any(marker in text for marker in transient_markers)
 
     def _process_tts_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
         if not self.tts_adapter_enabled:
             raise RuntimeError("tts adapter is disabled")
         attempts: List[str] = []
         for engine_name, adapter in self._select_tts_adapters():
             if not adapter.is_ready():
                 attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: not ready")
                 continue
             try:
                 result = adapter.process(task)
             except Exception as exc:
                 attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: {exc}")
                 continue
 
             output_path = str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
             if not output_path:
                 attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: empty output_path")
                 continue
             result = dict(result)
             result.setdefault("tts_engine_selected", engine_name)
             task.current_stage = 9
             task.stage_checkpoint = f"tts_{engine_name}_completed"
             return result
         raise RuntimeError("tts processing failed: " + " | ".join(attempts))
 
     def _select_tts_adapters(self) -> List[Tuple[str, Any]]:
         if self.tts_engine_mode == "http":
             return [("http", self.tts_http_adapter)]
         if self.tts_engine_mode == "auto":
             return [
                 ("local", self.tts_local_adapter),
                 ("http", self.tts_http_adapter),
             ]
         return [("local", self.tts_local_adapter)]
 
     def _process_video_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
         source_path = str(task.source_path or "").strip()
         use_internal = self.internal_pipeline_enabled or not self.video_adapter.is_enabled()
         if use_internal:
             if not source_path or not Path(source_path).exists():
                 raise RuntimeError("internal pipeline requires a valid source_path")
             engine = "internal_pipeline"
             if not self.internal_pipeline_enabled:
                 engine = "internal_pipeline_auto"
             result = self._run_internal_video_pipeline(task=task, source_path=source_path)
             result["engine"] = engine
             return result
 
         if self.video_adapter.is_enabled():
             result = self.video_adapter.process(task)
             task.current_stage = 9
             task.stage_checkpoint = "video_command"
             return result
 
         raise RuntimeError("no video engine configured")

     def _prepare_internal_pipeline_context(self, task: UnifiedTask, task_dir: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
         payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
         metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
         options: Dict[str, Any] = {}
 
         forum_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
         if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):

             forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})

             forum_post_info=forum_info,
             payload=payload,
             metadata=metadata,

         if forum_info:
             forum_post_info_path = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
             forum_post_info_path.write_text(
                 json.dumps(forum_info, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
                 encoding="utf-8",
             )
             options["forum_post_info_json"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
 
             next_metadata = dict(metadata)
             next_payload = dict(payload)
             next_metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
             next_metadata["internal_pipeline_forum_post_info_path"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
             next_payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
             task.metadata = next_metadata
             task.payload = next_payload
             metadata = next_metadata
             payload = next_payload
 
         stage5_model_name = self._pick_first_text(
             payload.get("stage5_model_name"),
             metadata.get("stage5_model_name"),
             payload.get("model_name"),
             metadata.get("model_name"),
         )
         if stage5_model_name:
             normalized_model, backend_model = self._normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(stage5_model_name)
             options["model"] = normalized_model
             if backend_model:
                 options["openai_backend_model"] = backend_model
 
         explicit_backend_model = self._pick_first_text(
             payload.get("openai_backend_model"),
             metadata.get("openai_backend_model"),
             payload.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
             metadata.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
         )
         if explicit_backend_model:
             options["openai_backend_model"] = explicit_backend_model
 
         file_encoding = self._pick_first_text(
             payload.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
             metadata.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
             payload.get("file_encoding"),
             metadata.get("file_encoding"),
         )
         if file_encoding:
             options["file_encoding"] = file_encoding
 
         stage5_use_preprocessor = self._extract_optional_bool(
             payload.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
             metadata.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
             payload.get("use_preprocessor"),
             metadata.get("use_preprocessor"),
         )
         if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
             options["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor

         )

     def _normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(self, model_name: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[str]]:
         raw_model = str(model_name or "").strip()
         if not raw_model:
             return "", None
 
         normalized = raw_model.lower()
         supported = {"openai", "qwen", "g4f", "deepseek", "kimi"}
         if normalized in supported:
             return normalized, None
 
         # Old stage5 only accepts provider ids. Route custom backend model ids
         # through the OpenAI-compatible adapter and pass the real backend via env.
         return "openai", raw_model
 
     def _collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs(self) -> List[str]:
         tool_dirs: List[str] = []
 
         explicit_dir = str(
             os.getenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "") or os.getenv("FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "")
         ).strip()
         if explicit_dir:
             candidate = Path(explicit_dir).expanduser().resolve()
             if candidate.exists():
                 tool_dirs.append(str(candidate))
 
         base_prefix = str(getattr(sys, "base_prefix", "") or "").strip()
         if base_prefix:
             prefix_path = Path(base_prefix).resolve()
             sibling_ffmpeg_dir = prefix_path.parent / "ffmpeg" / "bin"
             if sibling_ffmpeg_dir.exists():
                 tool_dirs.append(str(sibling_ffmpeg_dir))
 
         deduped: List[str] = []
         seen: set[str] = set()
         for item in tool_dirs:
             normalized = str(item).strip()
             if normalized and normalized not in seen:
                 seen.add(normalized)
                 deduped.append(normalized)
         return deduped
 
     def _append_internal_pipeline_args(self, cmd: List[str], pipeline_inputs: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
         model_name = str(pipeline_inputs.get("model") or "").strip()
         if model_name:
             cmd.extend(["--model", model_name])
 
         file_encoding = str(pipeline_inputs.get("file_encoding") or "").strip()
         if file_encoding:
             cmd.extend(["--file-encoding", file_encoding])
 
         if "stage5_use_preprocessor" in pipeline_inputs:
             if bool(pipeline_inputs["stage5_use_preprocessor"]):
                 cmd.append("--enable-preprocess")
             else:
                 cmd.append("--disable-preprocess")
 
         clip_text_file = str(pipeline_inputs.get("clip_text_file") or "").strip()
         if clip_text_file:
             cmd.extend(["--clip-text-file", clip_text_file])
 
         forum_post_info_json = str(pipeline_inputs.get("forum_post_info_json") or "").strip()
         if forum_post_info_json:
             cmd.extend(["--forum-post-info-json", forum_post_info_json])
 
         # Keep root artifacts for worker resolution instead of letting stage9 delete them.
         cmd.extend(["--organize-delete-original", "false"])
 
     def _build_internal_pipeline_env(self, pipeline_inputs: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, str]:
         env = dict(os.environ)
         path_entries: List[str] = []
 
         python_scripts_dir = Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent
         if python_scripts_dir.exists():
             path_entries.append(str(python_scripts_dir))
 
         path_entries.extend(self._collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs())
 
         current_path = str(env.get("PATH", "") or "")
         if current_path:
             path_entries.append(current_path)
         env["PATH"] = os.pathsep.join(path_entries)
 
         # Keep legacy pipeline subprocess I/O stable on Windows even when old
         # Rich logs emit emoji or non-ASCII text.
         env["PYTHONIOENCODING"] = "utf-8"
         env["PYTHONUTF8"] = "1"
 
         backend_model = ""
         if isinstance(pipeline_inputs, dict):
             backend_model = str(pipeline_inputs.get("openai_backend_model") or "").strip()
         if backend_model:
             env["OPENAI_BACKEND_MODEL"] = backend_model
         return env
 
     def _resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(self, task_dir: Path, source_path: Path) -> Path:
         state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
         if not state_file.exists():
             raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline state missing: {state_file}")
         try:
             payload = json.loads(state_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
         except Exception as exc:
             raise RuntimeError(f"parse internal pipeline state failed: {state_file}: {exc}") from exc
 
         last_completed_step = int(payload.get("last_completed_step", -1))
         if last_completed_step < 9:
             raise RuntimeError(
                 f"internal pipeline incomplete: last_completed_step={last_completed_step} state_file={state_file}"
             )

     def _safe_resolve_existing_path(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
         text = str(value or "").strip()
         if not text:
             return None
         candidate = Path(text)
         if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_file():
             return None
         try:
             return candidate.resolve()
         except Exception:
             return candidate
 
     def _safe_resolve_existing_dir(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
         text = str(value or "").strip()
         if not text:
             return None
         candidate = Path(text)
         if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_dir():
             return None
         try:
             return candidate.resolve()
         except Exception:
             return candidate
 
     def _should_expose_video_artifact(self, path: Path) -> bool:
         suffix = path.suffix.lower()
         name = path.name.lower()
         video_exts = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
         image_exts = {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}
         if suffix in video_exts or suffix in image_exts:
             return True
         if name in {"total.srt", "total.ass", "script.txt", "state.json"}:
             return True
         if name in {"clip_text.txt", "forum_post_info.json"}:
             return True
         if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in name:
             return True
         if suffix == ".log":
             return True
         return False
 
     def _classify_video_artifact_role(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[str, str]:
         text = path.name.lower()
         suffix = path.suffix.lower()
         if primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved:
             return "final_video", "video"
         if text == "total.srt":
             return "subtitle_srt", "subtitle"
         if text == "total.ass":
             return "subtitle_ass", "subtitle"
         if text == "script.txt":
             return "transcript_text", "transcript"
         if text == "clip_text.txt":
             return "clip_text", "text"
         if text == "forum_post_info.json":
             return "forum_post_info", "context"
         if text == "state.json":
             return "pipeline_state", "manifest"
         if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in text:
             return "cover_manifest", "manifest"
         if suffix == ".log":
             return "processing_log", "log"
         if suffix in {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}:
             return "cover_image", "image"
         if "无封面文字可自由添加" in path.name:
             return "coverless_video", "video"
         if "无字幕版" in path.name:
             return "video_no_subtitle", "video"
         if "带字幕版" in path.name:
             return "video_subtitled", "video"
         return "video", "video"
 
     def _video_artifact_sort_key(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[int, str]:
         role, _ = self._classify_video_artifact_role(path=path, primary_resolved=primary_resolved)
         order = {
             "final_video": 0,
             "video_subtitled": 1,
             "video_no_subtitle": 2,
             "coverless_video": 3,
             "subtitle_srt": 4,
             "subtitle_ass": 5,
             "transcript_text": 6,
             "clip_text": 7,
             "forum_post_info": 8,
             "cover_image": 9,
             "cover_manifest": 10,
             "processing_log": 11,
             "pipeline_state": 12,
             "video": 13,
         }
         return (order.get(role, 99), str(path).lower())
 
     def _build_video_artifact_id(self, role: str, index: int, used_ids: set[str]) -> str:
         base = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9]+", "_", str(role or "artifact").lower()).strip("_") or "artifact"
         candidate = base
         if candidate in used_ids:
             candidate = f"{base}_{index}"
         used_ids.add(candidate)
         return candidate

         if task_dir is None:

 def _parse_optional_bool(value: Any) -> bool | None:
     if value is None:
         return None
     if isinstance(value, bool):
         return value
     text = str(value).strip().lower()
     if not text:
         return None
     if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
         return True
     if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
         return False
     return None
 
 
 def _should_start_embedded_worker(cfg: Any) -> bool:
     env_value = _parse_optional_bool(os.getenv("CLONECUT_API_START_WORKER"))
     if env_value is not None:
         return env_value
 
     raw = getattr(cfg, "raw", None)
     if isinstance(raw, dict):
         api_cfg = raw.get("api", {}) or {}
         cfg_value = _parse_optional_bool(
             api_cfg.get("start_worker", api_cfg.get("start_embedded_worker"))
         )
         if cfg_value is not None:
             return cfg_value
 
     return False
 
 
 def create_app(service: WorkerService) -> Flask:
     app = Flask(
         __name__,
         template_folder=str(TEMPLATE_DIR),
         static_folder=str(STATIC_DIR),
         static_url_path="/web/static",
     )
     if app.jinja_loader is not None:
         app.jinja_loader = ChoiceLoader([app.jinja_loader, FileSystemLoader(str(TEMPLATE_DIR))])
 
     _api_token: str = os.getenv("CLONECUT_API_TOKEN", "").strip()
     _web_mock_mode = os.getenv("CLONECUT_WEB_MOCK_MODE", "").strip().lower() == "true"
     _api_upload_root = Path(getattr(service.config, "input_dir", "input")) / "_api_uploads"
     _api_upload_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 
     def _mock_mode_from_request() -> bool:
         if _web_mock_mode:
             return True
         raw = request.args.get("mock", "").strip().lower()
         return raw in {"1", "true", "yes"}
 
     def _parse_optional_bool(value: Any) -> Any:
         if value is None:
             return None
         if isinstance(value, bool):
             return value
         text = str(value).strip().lower()
         if not text:
             return None
         if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
             return True
         if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
             return False
         return None
 
     def _parse_json_object_field(field_name: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
         raw = str(request.form.get(field_name, "") or "").strip()
         if not raw:
             return {}
         try:
             parsed = json.loads(raw)
         except Exception as exc:
             raise ValueError(f"invalid {field_name}: {exc}") from exc
         if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
             raise ValueError(f"invalid {field_name}: expected JSON object")
         return dict(parsed)
 
     def _resolve_download_path(task: dict[str, Any]) -> Path | None:
         result = task.get("result") if isinstance(task.get("result"), dict) else {}
         artifacts = result.get("artifacts") if isinstance(result.get("artifacts"), list) else []
         for artifact in artifacts:
             if not isinstance(artifact, dict) or not artifact.get("is_primary"):
                 continue
             candidate = str(artifact.get("path") or "").strip()
             if not candidate:
                 continue
             path = Path(candidate)
             if path.exists() and path.is_file():
                 return path
         upload = result.get("upload") if isinstance(result.get("upload"), dict) else {}
         candidates = [
             str(upload.get("uploaded_path") or "").strip(),
             str(task.get("output_path") or "").strip(),
             str(result.get("named_output_path") or "").strip(),
             str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip(),
         ]
         for candidate in candidates:
             if not candidate:
                 continue
             path = Path(candidate)
             if path.exists() and path.is_file():
                 return path
         return None
 
     def _build_status_url(task_id: str) -> str:
         return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}"
 
     def _build_download_url(task_id: str) -> str:
         return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/download"
 
     def _build_artifacts_url(task_id: str) -> str:
         return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/artifacts"
 
     def _build_artifact_download_url(task_id: str, artifact_id: str) -> str:
         return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/artifacts/{artifact_id}/download"
 
     def _build_openclaw_result_url(task_id: str) -> str:
         return f"/api/tasks/{task_id}/openclaw-result"
 
     def _find_task_artifact(task: dict[str, Any], artifact_id: str) -> dict[str, Any] | None:
         result = task.get("result") if isinstance(task.get("result"), dict) else {}
         artifacts = result.get("artifacts") if isinstance(result.get("artifacts"), list) else []
         target = str(artifact_id or "").strip()
         if not target:
             return None
         for artifact in artifacts:
             if not isinstance(artifact, dict):
                 continue
             if str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip() == target:
                 return artifact
         return None
 
     def _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id: dict[str, dict[str, Any]], artifact_id: str) -> dict[str, Any] | None:
         target = str(artifact_id or "").strip()
         if not target:
             return None
         artifact = artifacts_by_id.get(target)
         if not isinstance(artifact, dict):
             return None
         return {
             "artifact_id": target,
             "role": artifact.get("role"),
             "kind": artifact.get("kind"),
             "filename": artifact.get("filename"),
             "path": artifact.get("path"),
             "relative_path": artifact.get("relative_path"),
             "download_url": artifact.get("download_url"),
             "is_primary": bool(artifact.get("is_primary")),
         }
 
     def _compact_json_like(value: Any) -> Any:
         if isinstance(value, dict):
             compacted: dict[str, Any] = {}
             for key, item in value.items():
                 normalized = _compact_json_like(item)
                 if normalized in (None, "", [], {}):
                     continue
                 compacted[str(key)] = normalized
             return compacted
         if isinstance(value, list):
             compacted_list = [_compact_json_like(item) for item in value]
             return [item for item in compacted_list if item not in (None, "", [], {})]
         return value
 
     def _build_openclaw_result(task: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
         decorated = _decorate_task_for_api(task, include_openclaw_result=False)
         task_id = str(decorated.get("task_id") or "").strip()
         result = decorated.get("result") if isinstance(decorated.get("result"), dict) else {}
         render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest") if isinstance(result.get("render_manifest"), dict) else {}
         artifacts = result.get("artifacts") if isinstance(result.get("artifacts"), list) else []
         artifacts_by_id = {
             str(item.get("artifact_id") or "").strip(): item
             for item in artifacts
             if isinstance(item, dict) and str(item.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
         }
         videos = render_manifest.get("videos") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("videos"), dict) else {}
         subtitles = render_manifest.get("subtitles") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("subtitles"), dict) else {}
         texts = render_manifest.get("texts") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("texts"), dict) else {}
         context = render_manifest.get("context") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("context"), dict) else {}
         cover = render_manifest.get("cover") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("cover"), dict) else {}
         logs = render_manifest.get("logs") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("logs"), dict) else {}
         pipeline_state = (
             render_manifest.get("pipeline_state") if isinstance(render_manifest.get("pipeline_state"), dict) else {}
         )
 
         openclaw_result = {
+            "schema_version": RESULT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
             "task_id": task_id,
             "status": decorated.get("status"),
             "is_ready": str(decorated.get("status") or "").strip().lower() == "completed",
             "executed_mode": result.get("executed_mode"),
             "status_url": decorated.get("status_url"),
             "download_url": decorated.get("download_url"),
             "artifacts_url": decorated.get("artifacts_url"),
             "progress": {
                 "current_stage": decorated.get("current_stage"),
                 "stage_checkpoint": decorated.get("stage_checkpoint"),
                 "last_completed_step": pipeline_state.get("last_completed_step"),
                 "last_completed_step_name": pipeline_state.get("last_completed_step_name"),
             },
             "outputs": {
                 "final_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("primary") or "")),
                 "subtitled_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("subtitled") or "")),
                 "no_subtitle_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("no_subtitle") or "")),
                 "coverless_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("coverless") or "")),
                 "alternate_video": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(videos.get("alternate") or "")),
                 "subtitle_srt": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(subtitles.get("srt") or "")),
                 "subtitle_ass": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(subtitles.get("ass") or "")),
                 "script_text": _artifact_ref_by_id(
                     artifacts_by_id,
                     str(texts.get("script") or subtitles.get("script") or ""),
                 ),
                 "clip_text": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(texts.get("clip_text") or "")),
                 "cover_image": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(cover.get("image") or "")),
                 "forum_post_info": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(context.get("forum_post_info") or "")),
                 "processing_log": _artifact_ref_by_id(artifacts_by_id, str(logs.get("processing") or "")),
             },
             "manifest": {
                 "primary_artifact_id": render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id"),
                 "primary_download_url": render_manifest.get("primary_download_url"),
                 "artifact_count": render_manifest.get("artifact_count"),
             },
         }
         return _compact_json_like(openclaw_result)
 
     def _decorate_task_for_api(task: dict[str, Any], include_openclaw_result: bool = False) -> dict[str, Any]:
         decorated = copy.deepcopy(task)
         task_id = str(decorated.get("task_id") or "").strip()
         if not task_id:
             return decorated
 
         decorated["status_url"] = _build_status_url(task_id)
         decorated["download_url"] = _build_download_url(task_id)
         decorated["artifacts_url"] = _build_artifacts_url(task_id)
         decorated["openclaw_result_url"] = _build_openclaw_result_url(task_id)
 
         result = decorated.get("result")
         if not isinstance(result, dict):
             if include_openclaw_result:
                 decorated["openclaw_result"] = _build_openclaw_result(decorated)
             return decorated
 
         artifacts = result.get("artifacts")
         if isinstance(artifacts, list):
             for artifact in artifacts:
                 if not isinstance(artifact, dict):
                     continue
                 artifact_id = str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
                 if artifact_id:
                     artifact["download_url"] = _build_artifact_download_url(task_id, artifact_id)
 
         render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest")
         if isinstance(render_manifest, dict):
             primary_artifact_id = str(render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id") or "").strip()
             if primary_artifact_id:
                 render_manifest["primary_download_url"] = _build_artifact_download_url(task_id, primary_artifact_id)
         if include_openclaw_result:
             decorated["openclaw_result"] = _build_openclaw_result(decorated)
         return decorated
 
     def _save_uploaded_video(task_id: str) -> tuple[Path, str, int]:
         uploaded = request.files.get("file")
         if uploaded is None:
             raise ValueError("missing file field")
         filename = secure_filename(str(uploaded.filename or "").strip()) or "video.mp4"
         suffix = Path(filename).suffix.lower()
         content_type = str(uploaded.content_type or "").strip().lower()
         allowed_suffixes = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
         if suffix and suffix not in allowed_suffixes and not content_type.startswith("video/"):
             raise ValueError(f"unsupported video file type: {suffix or content_type or 'unknown'}")
 
         task_dir = _api_upload_root / task_id
         task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
         target = task_dir / filename
         uploaded.save(str(target))
         size_bytes = target.stat().st_size
         if size_bytes <= 0:
             target.unlink(missing_ok=True)
             raise ValueError("uploaded file is empty")
         return target, filename, size_bytes
 
     def _build_upload_task_payload(task_id: str, source_path: Path, original_filename: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
         payload = _parse_json_object_field("payload")
         metadata = _parse_json_object_field("metadata")
         forum_post_info = _parse_json_object_field("forum_post_info")
 
         for key in ("clip_text", "stage5_model_name", "stage5_file_encoding", "post_url"):
             value = str(request.form.get(key, "") or "").strip()
             if value:
                 payload[key] = value
                 metadata[key] = value
 
         stage5_use_preprocessor = _parse_optional_bool(request.form.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"))
         if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
             payload["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor
             metadata["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor
 
         if forum_post_info:
             payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
             metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
 
         metadata.setdefault("source", str(request.form.get("source", "openclaw_upload")).strip() or "openclaw_upload")
         metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
         metadata["uploaded_via"] = "api_multipart"
 
         task_type = str(request.form.get("task_type", "video") or "video").strip() or "video"
         priority = str(request.form.get("priority", "normal") or "normal").strip() or "normal"

 def test_failed_task_auto_retries_until_success(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_retry.db"))
     cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
     service = WorkerService(cfg)
     source = tmp_path / "retry-source.mp4"
     source.write_bytes(b"video-content")
 
     original = service._process_video_like
     attempts = {"count": 0}
 
     def flaky_process(task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
         attempts["count"] += 1
         if attempts["count"] == 1:
             raise RuntimeError("inject process failure")
         return original(task)
 
     service._process_video_like = flaky_process  # type: ignore[method-assign]
 
     service.start()
     try:
         ok, task_id, error = service.submit(
             {
                 "task_type": "video",
                 "source_url": str(source),
                 "metadata": {"source": "retry-test"},
             }
         )
         assert ok
         assert not error
 
         deadline = time.time() + 15
         final_task = None
         while time.time() < deadline:
             final_task = service.get_task(task_id)
             if final_task and final_task.get("status") == "completed" and attempts["count"] >= 2:
                 break
             time.sleep(0.1)
 
         assert attempts["count"] >= 2
         assert isinstance(final_task, dict)
         assert final_task.get("status") == "completed"
         assert int(final_task.get("retry_count", 0)) >= 1
     finally:
         service.stop()

 def test_zombie_task_reclaimed_then_requeued(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_zombie.db"))
     cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
     service = WorkerService(cfg)
 
     zombie = UnifiedTask(
         task_id="zombie-1",
         task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
         source="unit",
         source_url=str(tmp_path / "missing.mp4"),
         status=TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
         current_stage=3,
         stage_checkpoint="stage3_repair",
         max_retries=1,
     )
     zombie.started_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=40)
     service._persist_task(zombie)
 
     reclaimed = service._reclaim_zombies_once()
     assert reclaimed == 1
 
     time.sleep(1.2)
     ready = service._dequeue_ready_retries()
     assert len(ready) == 1
     service._enqueue_retry_task(ready[0])
 
     queued = service.queue_adapter.pop_process(timeout=0.1)
     assert queued is not None
     assert queued.task_id == "zombie-1"
     loaded = service.get_task("zombie-1")
     assert isinstance(loaded, dict)
     assert loaded.get("status") == "pending"
 
 
 def test_zombie_reclaim_uses_status_specific_thresholds(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_zombie_threshold.db"))
     cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
     cfg.raw["worker"]["zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds"] = {
         "pending": 1,
         "downloading": 120,
         "processing": 120,
         "uploading": 120,
     }
     service = WorkerService(cfg)
 
     pending_task = UnifiedTask(
         task_id="pending-zombie-1",
         task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
         source="unit",
         source_url=str(tmp_path / "pending.mp4"),
         status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
     )
     pending_task.created_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=10)
     service._persist_task(pending_task)
 
     processing_task = UnifiedTask(
         task_id="processing-fresh-1",
         task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
         source="unit",
         source_url=str(tmp_path / "processing.mp4"),
         status=TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
     )
     processing_task.started_at = datetime.now() - timedelta(seconds=10)
     service._persist_task(processing_task)
 
     reclaimed = service._reclaim_zombies_once()
     assert reclaimed == 1
 
     pending_loaded = service.get_task("pending-zombie-1")
     processing_loaded = service.get_task("processing-fresh-1")
     assert isinstance(pending_loaded, dict)
     assert isinstance(processing_loaded, dict)
     assert pending_loaded.get("status") == TaskStatus.FAILED.value
     assert processing_loaded.get("status") == TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value

 def test_attach_video_render_manifest_collects_primary_subtitle_cover_and_state(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_render_manifest.db"))
     cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
     service = WorkerService(cfg)
 
     task_dir = Path(cfg.output_dir) / "render-manifest-task"
     task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 
     final_video = task_dir / "论坛样本_final.mp4"
     final_video.write_bytes(b"final-video")
     no_subtitle_video = task_dir / "论坛样本_智能剪辑无字幕版.mp4"
     no_subtitle_video.write_bytes(b"no-subtitle")
     subtitle_srt = task_dir / "total.srt"
     subtitle_srt.write_text("1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nhello\n", encoding="utf-8")
     subtitle_ass = task_dir / "total.ass"
     subtitle_ass.write_text("[Script Info]\n", encoding="utf-8")
     script_text = task_dir / "script.txt"
     script_text.write_text("原始识别文本", encoding="utf-8")
     clip_text = task_dir / "clip_text.txt"
     clip_text.write_text("裁剪文本", encoding="utf-8")
     forum_post_info = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
     forum_post_info.write_text('{"thread_id":"123"}', encoding="utf-8")
     cover_image = task_dir / "论坛封面标题.png"
     cover_image.write_bytes(b"png")
     logs_dir = task_dir / "logs"
     logs_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     process_log = logs_dir / "funclip_20260326_150000.log"
     process_log.write_text("pipeline ok", encoding="utf-8")
     state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
     state_file.write_text(
         json.dumps(
             {
                 "last_completed_step": 9,
                 "output_file": str(final_video),
                 "step_name": "文件整理",
             },
             ensure_ascii=False,
         ),
         encoding="utf-8",
     )
 
     task = UnifiedTask(
         task_id="render-manifest-task",
         task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
         source="unit",
         source_path=str(tmp_path / "source.mp4"),
     )
     Path(str(task.source_path)).write_bytes(b"source-video")
 
     result = service._attach_video_render_manifest(
         task,
         {
             "success": True,
             "request_type": "video",
             "engine": "internal_pipeline",
             "output_path": str(final_video),
         },
     )
 
     artifacts = result.get("artifacts") or []
     roles = {str(item.get("role")): item for item in artifacts}
     assert "final_video" in roles
     assert roles["final_video"].get("is_primary") is True
     assert "subtitle_srt" in roles
     assert "subtitle_ass" in roles
     assert "clip_text" in roles
     assert "forum_post_info" in roles
     assert "cover_image" in roles
     assert "processing_log" in roles
     assert "pipeline_state" in roles
 
     render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest") or {}
+    assert render_manifest.get("schema_version") == "1.0"
     assert render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id") == roles["final_video"].get("artifact_id")
     subtitles = render_manifest.get("subtitles") or {}
     assert subtitles.get("srt") == roles["subtitle_srt"].get("artifact_id")
     assert subtitles.get("ass") == roles["subtitle_ass"].get("artifact_id")
     texts = render_manifest.get("texts") or {}
     assert texts.get("clip_text") == roles["clip_text"].get("artifact_id")
     assert texts.get("script") == roles["transcript_text"].get("artifact_id")
     context = render_manifest.get("context") or {}
     assert context.get("forum_post_info") == roles["forum_post_info"].get("artifact_id")
     cover = render_manifest.get("cover") or {}
     assert cover.get("image") == roles["cover_image"].get("artifact_id")
     logs = render_manifest.get("logs") or {}
     assert logs.get("processing") == roles["processing_log"].get("artifact_id")
     pipeline_state = render_manifest.get("pipeline_state") or {}
     assert pipeline_state.get("last_completed_step") == 9
 
 
 def test_internal_pipeline_context_maps_custom_backend_model_to_openai(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_internal_context.db"))

     source = tmp_path / "context-source.mp4"
     source.write_bytes(b"video-content")
 
     task = UnifiedTask(
         task_id="context-task",
         task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
         source="unit",
         source_path=str(source),
         payload={"stage5_model_name": "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"},
         metadata={"source": "unit"},
     )
 
     options = service._prepare_internal_pipeline_context(task=task, task_dir=task_dir)
 
     assert options.get("model") == "openai"

 def test_internal_pipeline_env_forces_utf8_and_backend_override(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_internal_env.db"))
     ffmpeg_bin_dir = tmp_path / "ffmpeg-bin"
     ffmpeg_bin_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", str(ffmpeg_bin_dir))
     cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
     service = WorkerService(cfg)
 
     env = service._build_internal_pipeline_env(
         pipeline_inputs={"openai_backend_model": "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"}
     )
 
     assert env.get("PYTHONIOENCODING") == "utf-8"
     assert env.get("PYTHONUTF8") == "1"
     assert env.get("OPENAI_BACKEND_MODEL") == "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"
     assert str(Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent) in env.get("PATH", "")
     assert str(ffmpeg_bin_dir.resolve()) in env.get("PATH", "")

 from apps.api.openclaw_client import run_openclaw_video_task, submit_openclaw_video_task, wait_for_openclaw_result
 
 
 class _FakeResponse:
     def __init__(self, status_code: int, payload):
         self.status_code = status_code
         self._payload = payload
         self.text = str(payload)
 
     def json(self):
         return self._payload
 
 
 class _FakeSession:
     def __init__(self, post_responses=None, get_responses=None) -> None:
         self.post_responses = list(post_responses or [])
         self.get_responses = list(get_responses or [])
         self.post_calls = []
         self.get_calls = []
 
     def post(self, url, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
         self.post_calls.append({"url": url, **kwargs})
         if not self.post_responses:
             raise AssertionError("unexpected post call")
         return self.post_responses.pop(0)
 
     def get(self, url, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
         self.get_calls.append({"url": url, **kwargs})
         if not self.get_responses:
             raise AssertionError("unexpected get call")
         return self.get_responses.pop(0)
 
 
 def test_submit_openclaw_video_task_posts_expected_form(tmp_path) -> None:
     video = tmp_path / "sample.mp4"
     video.write_bytes(b"video")
     session = _FakeSession(
         post_responses=[
             _FakeResponse(
                 201,
                 {
                     "success": True,
                     "task_id": "task-123",
                     "openclaw_result_url": "/api/tasks/task-123/openclaw-result",
                 },
             )
         ]
     )
 
     payload = submit_openclaw_video_task(
         api_base="http://127.0.0.1:18100",
         video_path=video,
         api_token="token-1",
         stage5_model_name="yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4",
         extra_form={"metadata": {"source": "test"}},
         session=session,
     )
 
     assert payload.get("task_id") == "task-123"
     call = session.post_calls[0]
     assert call["url"] == "http://127.0.0.1:18100/api/tasks/upload-video"

 def test_worker_service_start_and_stop_controls_warm_runner(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "runner_lifecycle.db"))
     events: list[str] = []
 
     class FakeRunner:
         def __init__(self, **_kwargs) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
             events.append("runner_init")
 
         def start(self) -> None:
             events.append("runner_start")
 
         def stop(self) -> None:
             events.append("runner_stop")
 
     monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module, "InternalPipelineWarmRunner", FakeRunner)
 
     service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path, runner_mode="warm_process"))
     service.resource_monitor = SimpleNamespace(
         start=lambda: events.append("resource_start"),
         stop=lambda: events.append("resource_stop"),
     )
     monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_recover_stuck_tasks", lambda: 0)
     monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_restore_retry_schedule", lambda: 0)
     monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_spawn_workers", lambda *_args, **_kwargs: None)
 
     service.start()
     service.stop()
 
     assert events == [
         "runner_init",
         "runner_start",
         "resource_start",
         "runner_stop",
         "resource_stop",
     ]

 def test_stage5_rule_based_script_generation(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.delenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", raising=False)
     monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_MODEL", raising=False)
 
     source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
     source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
     out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
     stage_dir = out_dir / "v2" / "_stages"
     stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     srt = stage_dir / "v2_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
     srt.write_text(
         "\n".join(

 def test_stage5_merges_forum_keywords_when_enabled(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
     monkeypatch.delenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", raising=False)
     monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_MODEL", raising=False)
     monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_USE_FORUM_KEYWORDS", "true")
 
     source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
     source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
     out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
     stage_dir = out_dir / "v5_forum_on" / "_stages"
     stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
     srt = stage_dir / "v5_forum_on_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
     srt.write_text(
         "\n".join(
             [
                 "1",
                 "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                 "generic transcript sentence",
                 "",
             ]
         ),
         encoding="utf-8",
     )
 
     result = stage5_ai_text.run(
         input_video=str(source),
         output_dir=str(out_dir),
         task_id="v5_forum_on",
         forum_post_info={"hotwords": ["论坛词A", "论坛词B", "论坛词A"]},
     )
     assert result.success
     manifest = stage_dir / "v5_forum_on_stage5_ai_manifest.json"
     payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
     assert payload.get("use_forum_keywords") is True
     assert payload.get("forum_keyword_count") == 2
     assert payload.get("keywords")[:2] == ["论坛词A", "论坛词B"]

 1258:         statuses = [int(item) for item in re.findall(r"status\s*=?\s*(\d{3})", text)]
 1259:         if any(400 <= status < 500 for status in statuses):
 1260:             return False
 1261:         if any(status >= 500 for status in statuses):
 1262:             return True
 1263:         if "login failed" in text or "auth" in text or "permission" in text:
 1264:             return False
 1265:         transient_markers = (
 1266:             "timeout",
 1267:             "timed out",
 1268:             "connection",
 1269:             "network",
 1270:             "temporar",
 1271:             "exception",
 1272:             "status=0",
 1273:         )
 1274:         return any(marker in text for marker in transient_markers)
 1275: 
 1276:     def _process_tts_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 1277:         if not self.tts_adapter_enabled:
 1278:             raise RuntimeError("tts adapter is disabled")
 1279:         attempts: List[str] = []
 1280:         for engine_name, adapter in self._select_tts_adapters():
 1281:             if not adapter.is_ready():
 1282:                 attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: not ready")
 1283:                 continue
 1284:             try:
 1285:                 result = adapter.process(task)
 1286:             except Exception as exc:
 1287:                 attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: {exc}")
 1288:                 continue
 1289: 
 1290:             output_path = str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
 1291:             if not output_path:
 1292:                 attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: empty output_path")
 1293:                 continue
 1294:             result = dict(result)
 1295:             result.setdefault("tts_engine_selected", engine_name)
 1296:             task.current_stage = 9
 1297:             task.stage_checkpoint = f"tts_{engine_name}_completed"
 1298:             return result
 1299:         raise RuntimeError("tts processing failed: " + " | ".join(attempts))
 1300: 
 1301:     def _select_tts_adapters(self) -> List[Tuple[str, Any]]:
 1302:         if self.tts_engine_mode == "http":
 1303:             return [("http", self.tts_http_adapter)]
 1304:         if self.tts_engine_mode == "auto":
 1305:             return [
 1306:                 ("local", self.tts_local_adapter),
 1307:                 ("http", self.tts_http_adapter),
 1308:             ]
 1309:         return [("local", self.tts_local_adapter)]
 1310: 
 1311:     def _process_video_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 1312:         source_path = str(task.source_path or "").strip()
 1313:         use_internal = self.internal_pipeline_enabled or not self.video_adapter.is_enabled()
 1314:         if use_internal:
 1315:             if not source_path or not Path(source_path).exists():
 1316:                 raise RuntimeError("internal pipeline requires a valid source_path")
 1317:             engine = "internal_pipeline"
 1318:             if not self.internal_pipeline_enabled:
 1319:                 engine = "internal_pipeline_auto"
 1320:             result = self._run_internal_video_pipeline(task=task, source_path=source_path)
 1321:             result["engine"] = engine
 1322:             return result
 1323: 
 1324:         if self.video_adapter.is_enabled():
 1325:             result = self.video_adapter.process(task)
 1326:             task.current_stage = 9
 1327:             task.stage_checkpoint = "video_command"
 1328:             return result
 1329: 
 1330:         raise RuntimeError("no video engine configured")
 1331: 
 1332:     def _run_internal_video_pipeline(self, task: UnifiedTask, source_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 1333:         task_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / task.task_id
 1334:         task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 1335:         source = Path(source_path)
 1336:         if not source.exists():
 1337:             task.stage_checkpoint = "stage0_clean"
 1338:             task.current_stage = 0
 1339:             raise RuntimeError(f"source file not found: {source}")
 1340:         stage_names = [
 1341:             "stage0_clean",
 1342:             "stage1_transcode",
 1343:             "stage2_silence",
 1344:             "stage3_repair",
 1345:             "stage4_asr",
 1346:             "stage5_ai_text",
 1347:             "stage6_clip",
 1348:             "stage6_5_resub",
 1349:             "stage7_correct",
 1350:             "stage7_subtitle",
 1351:             "stage8_cover",
 1352:             "stage9_organize",
 1353:         ]
 1354:         start_from_stage = 0
 1355:         pipeline_inputs = self._prepare_internal_pipeline_context(task=task, task_dir=task_dir)
 1356: 
 1357:         if self._should_use_internal_pipeline_migration_fallback(source):
 1358:             return self._run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(
 1359:                 task=task,
 1360:                 source=source,
 1361:                 task_dir=task_dir,
 1362:                 stage_names=stage_names,
 1363:                 start_from_stage=start_from_stage,
 1364:                 reason="migration fallback: tiny input",
 1365:             )
 1366: 
 1367:         pipeline = VideoPipeline(
 1368:             config=VideoPipelineConfig.from_env(output_dir=str(self.config.output_dir)),
 1369:             logger=self.logger,
 1370:             performance_tracker=self.performance_tracker,
 1371:             resource_monitor=self.resource_monitor,
 1372:         )
 1373:         started = time.perf_counter()
 1374:         pipeline_result = pipeline.run(
 1375:             input_video=str(source),
 1376:             task_id=task.task_id,
 1377:             start_from_stage=start_from_stage,
 1378:             forum_post_info=dict(task.metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
 1379:             if isinstance(task.metadata, dict)
 1380:             else {},
 1381:         )
 1382:         elapsed_ms = int(max(0.0, (time.perf_counter() - started) * 1000))
 1383: 
 1384:         checkpoint = str(pipeline_result.last_stage or pipeline_result.failed_stage or "").strip()
 1385:         if checkpoint:
 1386:             task.stage_checkpoint = checkpoint
 1387:         task.current_stage = int(getattr(pipeline_result, "current_stage", start_from_stage))
 1388: 
 1389:         output_path = str(getattr(pipeline_result, "output_file", "") or "").strip()
 1390:         self._write_internal_pipeline_state(
 1391:             task_dir=task_dir,
 1392:             output_path=output_path,
 1393:             stage_name=checkpoint,
 1394:             current_stage=task.current_stage,
 1395:         )
 1396: 
 1397:         if not bool(getattr(pipeline_result, "success", False)):
 1398:             error_message = str(getattr(pipeline_result, "error_message", "") or "").strip()
 1399:             raise RuntimeError(error_message or "video pipeline failed")
 1400: 
 1401:         return {
 1402:             "success": True,
 1403:             "request_type": task.task_type.value,
 1404:             "output_path": output_path,
 1405:             "executed_stages": list(getattr(pipeline_result, "executed_stages", []) or []),
 1406:             "executed_mode": "video_pipeline",
 1407:             "performance_summary": (
 1408:                 str(getattr(pipeline_result, "performance_summary", "") or "").strip()
 1409:                 or f"video pipeline executed duration_ms={elapsed_ms}"
 1410:             ),
 1411:         }
 1412: 
 1413:     def _should_use_internal_pipeline_migration_fallback(self, source: Path) -> bool:
 1414:         threshold_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("internal_pipeline_migration_fallback_max_bytes", 0)
 1415:         try:
 1416:             threshold = max(0, int(threshold_raw))
 1417:         except Exception:
 1418:             threshold = 0
 1419:         if threshold <= 0:
 1420:             return False
 1421:         try:
 1422:             return source.stat().st_size <= threshold
 1423:         except Exception:
 1424:             return False

 1426:     def _write_internal_pipeline_state(
 1427:         self,
 1428:         *,
 1429:         task_dir: Path,
 1430:         output_path: str,
 1431:         stage_name: str,
 1432:         current_stage: int,
 1433:     ) -> None:
 1434:         step_mapping = {
 1435:             "stage0_clean": 0,
 1436:             "stage1_transcode": 1,
 1437:             "stage2_silence": 2,
 1438:             "stage3_repair": 3,
 1439:             "stage4_asr": 4,
 1440:             "stage5_ai_text": 5,
 1441:             "stage6_clip": 6,
 1442:             "stage6_5_resub": 6,
 1443:             "stage7_correct": 7,
 1444:             "stage7_subtitle": 7,
 1445:             "stage8_cover": 8,
 1446:             "stage9_organize": 9,
 1447:         }
 1448:         payload = {
 1449:             "last_completed_step": int(step_mapping.get(stage_name, max(0, current_stage))),
 1450:             "last_completed_step_name": stage_name,
 1451:             "output_file": output_path,
 1452:         }
 1453:         state_path = task_dir / "state.json"
 1454:         state_path.write_text(
 1455:             json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
 1456:             encoding="utf-8",
 1457:         )

 1459:     def _prepare_internal_pipeline_context(self, task: UnifiedTask, task_dir: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 1460:         payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
 1461:         metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
 1462:         options: Dict[str, Any] = {}
 1463: 
 1464:         forum_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
 1465:         if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
 1466:             forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
 1467:         if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
 1468:             forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
 1469:

 1471:             forum_post_info=forum_info,
 1472:             payload=payload,
 1473:             metadata=metadata,
 1474:             source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
 1475:         )

 1477:             forum_info["original_filename"] = original_filename
 1478:

 1481:             forum_post_info_path.write_text(
 1482:                 json.dumps(forum_info, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
 1483:                 encoding="utf-8",
 1484:             )
 1485:             options["forum_post_info_json"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
 1486: 
 1487:             next_metadata = dict(metadata)
 1488:             next_payload = dict(payload)
 1489:             next_metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
 1490:             next_metadata["internal_pipeline_forum_post_info_path"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
 1491:             next_payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
 1492:             task.metadata = next_metadata
 1493:             task.payload = next_payload
 1494:             metadata = next_metadata
 1495:             payload = next_payload
 1496: 
 1497:         stage5_model_name = self._pick_first_text(
 1498:             payload.get("stage5_model_name"),
 1499:             metadata.get("stage5_model_name"),
 1500:             payload.get("model_name"),
 1501:             metadata.get("model_name"),
 1502:         )
 1503:         if stage5_model_name:
 1504:             normalized_model, backend_model = self._normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(stage5_model_name)
 1505:             options["model"] = normalized_model
 1506:             if backend_model:
 1507:                 options["openai_backend_model"] = backend_model
 1508: 
 1509:         explicit_backend_model = self._pick_first_text(
 1510:             payload.get("openai_backend_model"),
 1511:             metadata.get("openai_backend_model"),
 1512:             payload.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
 1513:             metadata.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
 1514:         )
 1515:         if explicit_backend_model:
 1516:             options["openai_backend_model"] = explicit_backend_model
 1517: 
 1518:         file_encoding = self._pick_first_text(
 1519:             payload.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
 1520:             metadata.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
 1521:             payload.get("file_encoding"),
 1522:             metadata.get("file_encoding"),
 1523:         )
 1524:         if file_encoding:
 1525:             options["file_encoding"] = file_encoding
 1526: 
 1527:         stage5_use_preprocessor = self._extract_optional_bool(
 1528:             payload.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
 1529:             metadata.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
 1530:             payload.get("use_preprocessor"),
 1531:             metadata.get("use_preprocessor"),
 1532:         )
 1533:         if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
 1534:             options["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor
 1535: 
 1536:         clip_text = self._pick_first_text(
 1537:             payload.get("clip_text"),
 1538:             metadata.get("clip_text"),
 1539:         )
 1540:         if clip_text:
 1541:             clip_text_path = task_dir / "clip_text.txt"
 1542:             clip_text_path.write_text(clip_text, encoding="utf-8")
 1543:             options["clip_text_file"] = str(clip_text_path)
 1544:         else:
 1545:             clip_text_file = self._pick_first_text(
 1546:                 payload.get("clip_text_file"),
 1547:                 metadata.get("clip_text_file"),
 1548:             )
 1549:             if clip_text_file and Path(clip_text_file).exists():
 1550:                 options["clip_text_file"] = clip_text_file
 1551: 
 1552:         return options
 1553: 
 1554:     def _normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(self, model_name: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[str]]:
 1555:         raw_model = str(model_name or "").strip()
 1556:         if not raw_model:
 1557:             return "", None
 1558: 
 1559:         normalized = raw_model.lower()
 1560:         supported = {"openai", "qwen", "g4f", "deepseek", "kimi"}
 1561:         if normalized in supported:
 1562:             return normalized, None
 1563: 
 1564:         # Old stage5 only accepts provider ids. Route custom backend model ids
 1565:         # through the OpenAI-compatible adapter and pass the real backend via env.
 1566:         return "openai", raw_model
