 1487:     def _prepare_internal_pipeline_context(self, task: UnifiedTask, task_dir: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 1488:         payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
 1489:         metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
 1490:         options: Dict[str, Any] = {}
 1491: 
 1492:         forum_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
 1493:         if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
 1494:             forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
 1495:         if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
 1496:             forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
 1497: 
 1498:         original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
 1499:             forum_post_info=forum_info,
 1500:             payload=payload,
 1501:             metadata=metadata,
 1502:             source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
 1503:         )
 1504:         if original_filename:
 1505:             forum_info["original_filename"] = original_filename
 1506: 
 1507:         if forum_info:
 1508:             forum_post_info_path = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
 1509:             forum_post_info_path.write_text(
 1510:                 json.dumps(forum_info, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
 1511:                 encoding="utf-8",
 1512:             )
 1513:             options["forum_post_info_json"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
 1514: 
 1515:             next_metadata = dict(metadata)
 1516:             next_payload = dict(payload)
 1517:             next_metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
 1518:             next_metadata["internal_pipeline_forum_post_info_path"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
 1519:             next_payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
 1520:             task.metadata = next_metadata
 1521:             task.payload = next_payload
 1522:             metadata = next_metadata
 1523:             payload = next_payload
 1524: 
 1525:         stage5_model_name = self._pick_first_text(
 1526:             payload.get("stage5_model_name"),
 1527:             metadata.get("stage5_model_name"),
 1528:             payload.get("model_name"),
 1529:             metadata.get("model_name"),
 1530:         )
 1531:         if stage5_model_name:
 1532:             normalized_model, backend_model = self._normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(stage5_model_name)
 1533:             options["model"] = normalized_model
 1534:             if backend_model:
 1535:                 options["openai_backend_model"] = backend_model
 1536: 
 1537:         explicit_backend_model = self._pick_first_text(
 1538:             payload.get("openai_backend_model"),
 1539:             metadata.get("openai_backend_model"),
 1540:             payload.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
 1541:             metadata.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
 1542:         )
 1543:         if explicit_backend_model:
 1544:             options["openai_backend_model"] = explicit_backend_model
 1545: 
 1546:         file_encoding = self._pick_first_text(
 1547:             payload.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
 1548:             metadata.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
 1549:             payload.get("file_encoding"),
 1550:             metadata.get("file_encoding"),
 1551:         )
 1552:         if file_encoding:
 1553:             options["file_encoding"] = file_encoding
 1554: 
 1555:         stage5_use_preprocessor = self._extract_optional_bool(
 1556:             payload.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
 1557:             metadata.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
 1558:             payload.get("use_preprocessor"),
 1559:             metadata.get("use_preprocessor"),
 1560:         )
 1561:         if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
 1562:             options["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor
 1563: 
 1564:         clip_text = self._pick_first_text(
 1565:             payload.get("clip_text"),
 1566:             metadata.get("clip_text"),
 1567:         )
 1568:         if clip_text:
 1569:             clip_text_path = task_dir / "clip_text_input.txt"
 1570:             clip_text_path.write_text(clip_text, encoding="utf-8")
 1571:             options["clip_text_file"] = str(clip_text_path)
 1572:         else:
 1573:             clip_text_file = self._pick_first_text(
 1574:                 payload.get("clip_text_file"),
 1575:                 metadata.get("clip_text_file"),
 1576:             )
 1577:             if clip_text_file and Path(clip_text_file).exists():
 1578:                 options["clip_text_file"] = clip_text_file
 1579: 
 1580:         return options
 1581: 
 1582:     def _normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(self, model_name: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[str]]:
 1583:         raw_model = str(model_name or "").strip()
 1584:         if not raw_model:
 1585:             return "", None
 1586: 
 1587:         normalized = raw_model.lower()
 1588:         supported = {"openai", "qwen", "g4f", "deepseek", "kimi"}
 1589:         if normalized in supported:
 1590:             return normalized, None
 1591: 
 1592:         # Old stage5 only accepts provider ids. Route custom backend model ids
 1593:         # through the OpenAI-compatible adapter and pass the real backend via env.
 1594:         return "openai", raw_model
 1595: 
 1596:     def _collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs(self) -> List[str]:
 1597:         tool_dirs: List[str] = []
 1598: 
 1599:         explicit_dir = str(
 1600:             os.getenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "") or os.getenv("FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "")
 1601:         ).strip()
 1602:         if explicit_dir:
 1603:             candidate = Path(explicit_dir).expanduser().resolve()
 1604:             if candidate.exists():
 1605:                 tool_dirs.append(str(candidate))
 1606: 
 1607:         base_prefix = str(getattr(sys, "base_prefix", "") or "").strip()
 1608:         if base_prefix:
 1609:             prefix_path = Path(base_prefix).resolve()
 1610:             sibling_ffmpeg_dir = prefix_path.parent / "ffmpeg" / "bin"
 1611:             if sibling_ffmpeg_dir.exists():
 1612:                 tool_dirs.append(str(sibling_ffmpeg_dir))
 1613: 
 1614:         deduped: List[str] = []
 1615:         seen: set[str] = set()
 1616:         for item in tool_dirs:
 1617:             normalized = str(item).strip()
 1618:             if normalized and normalized not in seen:
 1619:                 seen.add(normalized)
 1620:                 deduped.append(normalized)
 1621:         return deduped
 1622: 
 1623:     def _append_internal_pipeline_args(self, cmd: List[str], pipeline_inputs: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
 1624:         model_name = str(pipeline_inputs.get("model") or "").strip()
 1625:         if model_name:
 1626:             cmd.extend(["--model", model_name])
 1627: 
 1628:         file_encoding = str(pipeline_inputs.get("file_encoding") or "").strip()
 1629:         if file_encoding:
 1630:             cmd.extend(["--file-encoding", file_encoding])
 1631: 
 1632:         if "stage5_use_preprocessor" in pipeline_inputs:
 1633:             if bool(pipeline_inputs["stage5_use_preprocessor"]):
 1634:                 cmd.append("--enable-preprocess")
 1635:             else:
 1636:                 cmd.append("--disable-preprocess")
 1637: 
 1638:         clip_text_file = str(pipeline_inputs.get("clip_text_file") or "").strip()
 1639:         if clip_text_file:
 1640:             cmd.extend(["--clip-text-file", clip_text_file])
 1641: 
 1642:         forum_post_info_json = str(pipeline_inputs.get("forum_post_info_json") or "").strip()
 1643:         if forum_post_info_json:
 1644:             cmd.extend(["--forum-post-info-json", forum_post_info_json])
 1645: 
 1646:         # Keep root artifacts for worker resolution instead of letting stage9 delete them.
 1647:         cmd.extend(["--organize-delete-original", "false"])
 1648: 
 1649:     def _build_internal_pipeline_env(self, pipeline_inputs: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, str]:
 1650:         env = dict(os.environ)
 1651:         path_entries: List[str] = []
 1652: 
 1653:         python_scripts_dir = Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent
 1654:         if python_scripts_dir.exists():
 1655:             path_entries.append(str(python_scripts_dir))
 1656: 
 1657:         path_entries.extend(self._collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs())
 1658: 
 1659:         current_path = str(env.get("PATH", "") or "")
 1660:         if current_path:
 1661:             path_entries.append(current_path)
 1662:         env["PATH"] = os.pathsep.join(path_entries)
 1663: 
 1664:         # Keep legacy pipeline subprocess I/O stable on Windows even when old
 1665:         # Rich logs emit emoji or non-ASCII text.
 1666:         env["PYTHONIOENCODING"] = "utf-8"
 1667:         env["PYTHONUTF8"] = "1"
 1668: 
 1669:         backend_model = ""
 1670:         if isinstance(pipeline_inputs, dict):
 1671:             backend_model = str(pipeline_inputs.get("openai_backend_model") or "").strip()
 1672:         if backend_model:
 1673:             env["OPENAI_BACKEND_MODEL"] = backend_model
 1674:         return env
 1675: 
 1676:     def _resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(self, task_dir: Path, source_path: Path) -> Path:
 1677:         state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
 1678:         if not state_file.exists():
 1679:             raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline state missing: {state_file}")
 1680:         try:
 1681:             payload = json.loads(state_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 1682:         except Exception as exc:
 1683:             raise RuntimeError(f"parse internal pipeline state failed: {state_file}: {exc}") from exc
 1684: 
 1685:         last_completed_step = int(payload.get("last_completed_step", -1))
 1686:         if last_completed_step < 9:
 1687:             raise RuntimeError(
 1688:                 f"internal pipeline incomplete: last_completed_step={last_completed_step} state_file={state_file}"
 1689:             )
 1690:         output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
 1691:         if output_file:
 1692:             candidate = Path(output_file)
 1693:             if candidate.exists():
 1694:                 return candidate
 1695: 
 1696:         patterns = [
 1697:             f"{source_path.stem}*_智能剪辑带字幕版*.mp4",
 1698:             "*_智能剪辑带字幕版*.mp4",
 1699:             "*.mp4",
 1700:         ]
 1701:         for pattern in patterns:
 1702:             candidates = [
 1703:                 p for p in task_dir.rglob(pattern)
 1704:                 if p.is_file() and "_stages" not in p.parts and "debug" not in p.parts
 1705:             ]
 1706:             if candidates:
 1707:                 candidates.sort(key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime, reverse=True)
 1708:                 return candidates[0]
 1709: 
 1710:         raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline produced no video output under: {task_dir}")
 1711: 
 1712:     def _run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(

 1757:             "success": True,

 1760:             "executed_stages": executed,

from __future__ import annotations

import multiprocessing
import os
from concurrent.futures import ProcessPoolExecutor
from concurrent.futures.process import BrokenProcessPool
from pathlib import Path
from threading import RLock
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional


def _reconfigure_stdio_utf8() -> None:
    for stream_name in ("stdout", "stderr"):
        stream = getattr(os.sys, stream_name, None)
        if stream is None:
            continue
        reconfigure = getattr(stream, "reconfigure", None)
        if callable(reconfigure):
            try:
                reconfigure(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
            except Exception:
                continue


def _apply_env(overrides: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> Dict[str, Optional[str]]:
    snapshot: Dict[str, Optional[str]] = {}
    for key, value in (overrides or {}).items():
        snapshot[key] = os.environ.get(key)
        if value:
            os.environ[key] = str(value)
        elif key in os.environ:
            os.environ.pop(key, None)
    return snapshot


def _restore_env(snapshot: Dict[str, Optional[str]]) -> None:
    for key, value in snapshot.items():
        if value is None:
            os.environ.pop(key, None)
        else:
            os.environ[key] = value


def _set_repo_root(repo_root: str) -> str:
    resolved = str(Path(repo_root).resolve())
    if resolved not in os.sys.path:
        os.sys.path.insert(0, resolved)
    os.chdir(resolved)
    return resolved


def _child_initializer(repo_root: str, base_env: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> None:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _apply_env(base_env)
    _set_repo_root(repo_root)


def _warmup_job(payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _set_repo_root(str(payload["repo_root"]))
    env_snapshot = _apply_env(payload.get("env"))
    try:
        from domain.video.pre.main import pipeline as pipeline_module

        warmed = pipeline_module.warm_pipeline_runtime(output_dir=str(payload["output_dir"]))
        return {"warmed": bool(warmed)}
    finally:
        _restore_env(env_snapshot)


def _execute_pipeline_job(payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _set_repo_root(str(payload["repo_root"]))
    env_snapshot = _apply_env(payload.get("env"))
    try:
        from domain.video.pre.main import pipeline as pipeline_module

        success = pipeline_module.run_pipeline_request(
            input_path=str(payload["input_path"]),
            output_dir=str(payload["output_dir"]),
            model=payload.get("model"),
            file_encoding=payload.get("file_encoding"),
            enable_preprocess=bool(payload.get("enable_preprocess", False)),
            disable_preprocess=bool(payload.get("disable_preprocess", False)),
            clip_text=payload.get("clip_text"),
            clip_text_file=payload.get("clip_text_file"),
            forum_post_info_json=payload.get("forum_post_info_json"),
            organize_delete_original=payload.get("organize_delete_original"),
        )
        if not success:
            raise RuntimeError("warm internal pipeline returned False")
        return {"success": True}
    finally:
        _restore_env(env_snapshot)


class InternalPipelineWarmRunner:
    def __init__(
        self,
        *,
        repo_root: str,
        output_dir: str,
        pool_size: int = 1,
        warmup_on_start: bool = True,
        base_env: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None,
        logger: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.repo_root = str(Path(repo_root).resolve())
        self.output_dir = str(Path(output_dir).resolve())
        self.pool_size = max(1, int(pool_size))
        self.warmup_on_start = bool(warmup_on_start)
        self.base_env = dict(base_env or {})
        self.logger = logger
        self._executor: Optional[ProcessPoolExecutor] = None
        self._lock = RLock()

    def start(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            if self._executor is not None:
                return
            context = multiprocessing.get_context("spawn")
            self._executor = ProcessPoolExecutor(
                max_workers=self.pool_size,
                mp_context=context,
                initializer=_child_initializer,
                initargs=(self.repo_root, self.base_env),
            )
            if self.warmup_on_start:
                for _ in range(self.pool_size):
                    self._executor.submit(
                        _warmup_job,
                        {
                            "repo_root": self.repo_root,
                            "output_dir": self.output_dir,
                            "env": {},
                        },
                    )
            if self.logger is not None:
                self.logger.info(
                    "internal warm runner started: pool_size=%s warmup_on_start=%s",
                    self.pool_size,
                    self.warmup_on_start,
                )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            executor = self._executor
            self._executor = None
        if executor is not None:
            executor.shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True)
            if self.logger is not None:
                self.logger.info("internal warm runner stopped")

    def execute(self, *, payload: Dict[str, Any], timeout_seconds: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if self._executor is None:
            self.start()
        executor = self._executor
        if executor is None:
            raise RuntimeError("warm runner executor unavailable")

        try:
            future = executor.submit(_execute_pipeline_job, payload)
            return future.result(timeout=timeout_seconds)
        except BrokenProcessPool as exc:
            self.stop()
            raise RuntimeError(f"warm runner process pool broke: {exc}") from exc

Issues (Critical/Important/Minor)

Critical:
1. 用户传入的 clip_text 会被 stage5 无条件覆盖，导致 stage6 读不到用户原始裁剪文本（cutover 后行为回归风险高）。

Important:
1. Worker 仍构建/启动 InternalPipelineWarmRunner，但执行路径已完全不使用它，造成边界不清和潜在资源浪费。
参考 [apps/worker/service.py#L246](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L246), [apps/worker/service.py#L273](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L273), [apps/worker/service.py#L1332](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1332)。
2. _prepare_internal_pipeline_context 解析出的 model/file_encoding/stage5_use_preprocessor/openai_backend_model 没有传入 VideoPipeline，只剩“形状兼容”，语义兼容弱。
参考 [apps/worker/service.py#L1355](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1355), [apps/worker/service.py#L1374](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1374), [apps/worker/service.py#L1497](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1497)。
3. state.json 映射存在脆弱点：last_stage/failed_stage 直接映射为 last_completed_step，失败时可能把失败步骤记成已完成；且未知 stage 回退到 current_stage（可能超出旧 0-9 语义）。
参考 [apps/worker/service.py#L1384](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1384), [apps/worker/service.py#L1449](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1449)。

Minor:
1. 仍留有旧路径残留（未使用 import/方法），会增加维护噪音。
参考 [apps/worker/service.py#L5](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L5), [apps/worker/service.py#L12](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L12), [apps/worker/service.py#L1595](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1595), [apps/worker/service.py#L1648](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/worker/service.py#L1648)。
2. 测试里还有旧 funasr monkeypatch 夹杂（与新主路径无关），针对性可再收紧。
参考 [tests/unit/test_worker_service.py#L23](/C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/tests/unit/test_worker_service.py#L23)。
